[LLM ANSWER]
**Stress at Work Questionnaire**

**Section 1: Perceived Stress Levels**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how often do you feel stressed at work?

(1 = Rarely, 2 = Occasionally, 3 = Frequently, 4 = Almost always, 5 = Almost never)

2. How would you rate the overall stress level in your current role?

(1 = Low, 2 = Moderate, 3 = High, 4 = Very High, 5 = Extremely High)

**Section 2: Triggers and Coping Mechanisms**

3. What are some common situations or events that cause you to feel stressed at work? (Check all that apply)

* Tight deadlines
* Heavy workload
* Conflicting priorities
* Lack of resources
* Communication issues
* Other (please specify)

4. How do you typically cope with stress at work?

(Select all that apply)

* Taking a break or stepping away from the situation
* Talking to a colleague or supervisor
* Practicing deep breathing or relaxation techniques
* Engaging in physical activity or exercise
* Seeking support from a mental health professional
* Other (please specify)

**Section 3: Impact on Well-being**

5. How has stress at work affected your overall well-being?

(Select all that apply)

* Negative impact on mood
* Increased anxiety or depression
* Physical symptoms (e.g. headaches, fatigue)
* Difficulty sleeping or concentrating
* Other (please specify)

6. Have you experienced any physical symptoms related to stress at work? If yes, please describe.

7. Are there any changes or interventions that would help you manage stress at work more effectively? If yes, please describe.

Thank you for taking the time to complete this questionnaire! Your responses will help us better understand stress at work and identify potential solutions.

```
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat confident"},
              {"ANSWER": "Neutral"},
              {"ANSWER": "Not very confident"},
              {"ANSWER": "Not at all confident"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "q9",
            "NAME": "What would you like to see changed or improved in terms of career development opportunities within the company?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 9,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": []
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

Note that I've used the `TYPE_ID` values to determine the type of question, and the `_TF_ANSWERS` arrays to store the possible answers for each question.
